          <h2 class="core-section-container__title section-title">
            Hakkƒ±mƒ±zda
          </h2>

<!---->
      <div class="core-section-container__content break-words">
        

          <p class="break-words text-color-text" data-test-id="about-us__description">
              Virgosol is a next-gen QA &amp; Software Testing Services provider co-headquartered in Istanbul and offshore test labs around Turkey in 5 different cities. Virgosol testing services covers Test Consultancy and Management, Functional and Non-Functional testing, Test Automation, DevOps, Agile, Web, Mobility and WebService/API to name a few. Virgosol is pioneering the next-gen Continuous Testing practices with a team of young, passionate testers focused on test automation, CI/ CD and shift left methodologies. With its in-house testing solutions, global pool of skilled testers, specialist testing approach and global delivery model, Virgosol is helping its clients transform their QA function to reduce production defects, reduce QA cycle times and lower overall QA costs. Virgosol has proven record of implementing projects in stipulated time frames &amp; budget with a team of experienced test professionals having rich experience in technology as well as vertical domains.

 

Our Vision

To become a trustworthy business that stands out for its innovative approach in the digital world, offering services on a global scale, and being favored by both clients and employees.


Our Mission

To design solutions that guide the industry by following international standards and technological developments. To provide sustainable services with happy employees by investing in continuous development and intellectual capital. To create the most efficient business models by prioritizing customer needs.


Our Services

- Software Test Consultancy

- Functional and Non-Functional Testing as A Service

- Regression Testing Service

- Performance Testing Service

- Test Automation Service

- Code Analysis and Test Coverage Measurement

- Web Service and API Testing Service

- Mobile Application Testing Service

- DevOps Consulting

- Training Services

- Outsourcing Services
          </p>

          Loadmance 
        
          </h3>
          

            <h4 class="base-main-card__subtitle body-text text-color-text overflow-hidden
                ">
              
            <a class="link-styled z-1" href="https://www.linkedin.com/products/categories/load-testing-software?trk=organization_guest_main_product_card_category_link" aria-label="LinkedIn‚Äòde Y√ºk Testi Yazƒ±lƒ±mƒ± g√∂r√ºnt√ºleyin" data-tracking-control-name="organization_guest_main_product_card_category_link" data-tracking-will-navigate>
              Y√ºk Testi Yazƒ±lƒ±mƒ±
            </a>
        
            </h4>

                <p class="base-main-card__description body-text text-color-text ">
                  
          Loadmance is a visual performance modeling, testing and result analysis platform where users can run performance testing scripts to test their web applications against heavy load, concurrent and multiple user traffic. 
With Loadmance:
- Testers and developers will be able to model and simulate how resources such as CPU and memory are consumed by the application.
- Different test runs can be compared to see the effects of system adjustments on performance.
-Customized dashboards can be created by selecting the desired parameters.
-Test runs can be scheduled for further use and can run automatically when the time comes
- The logs created based on the performance test can be downloaded.

        
                </p>
